Jamming detection report type enum

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If the reported status is the final status (end of the procedure), this shall be indicated within the status report. 

Other reports, called intermediate reports, gives only intermediate results issuing from the algorithm 
\end{DoxyNote}

\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+\+Add\+Preferred\+Operator(const char $\ast$\+L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+N\+N\+U\+L\+L mcc, const char $\ast$\+L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+N\+N\+U\+L\+L mnc, le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+\+Rat\+Bit\+Mask\+\_\+t rat\+Mask)}{le_mrc_AddPreferredOperator(const char *LE_NONNULL mcc, const char *LE_NONNULL mnc, le_mrc_RatBitMask_t ratMask)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf le\+\_\+result\+\_\+t} le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+\+Add\+Preferred\+Operator (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{const char $\ast$L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+N\+N\+U\+LL}]{mcc, }
\item[{const char $\ast$L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+N\+N\+U\+LL}]{mnc, }

Add a preferred operator by specifying the M\+C\+C/\+M\+NC and the Radio Access Technology.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+U\+N\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+ED List of User Preferred operators not available.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT Function failed.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+B\+A\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER R\+AT mask is invalid.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK Function succeeded.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If strings are not set, too long (bigger than L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+R\+C\+\_\+\+M\+C\+C\+\_\+\+L\+E\+N/\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+R\+C\+\_\+\+M\+N\+C\+\_\+\+L\+EN digits), or too short (less than L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+R\+C\+\_\+\+M\+C\+C\+\_\+\+L\+E\+N/\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+R\+C\+\_\+\+M\+N\+C\+\_\+\+L\+E\+N-\/1 digits) it\textquotesingle{}s a fatal error, the function won\textquotesingle{}t return.

{\bfseries N\+OT multi-\/app safe} 
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em mcc} & Mobile Country Code \\

\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em mnc} & Mobile Network Code \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em rat\+Mask} & Bit mask for the Radio Access Technology preferences. \\

\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{le__mrc__interface_8h_aa19103931ad3974ee014f0ce2705a4ff}{}\label{le__mrc__interface_8h_aa19103931ad3974ee014f0ce2705a4ff}
Connect the current client thread to the service providing this A\+PI. Block until the service is available.

For each thread that wants to use this A\+PI, either Connect\+Service or Try\+Connect\+Service must be called before any other functions in this A\+PI. Normally, Connect\+Service is automatically called for the main thread, but not for any other thread. For details, see \hyperlink{apiFilesC_apiFilesC_client}{Client-\/specific Functions}.

This function returns the signal metrics measured on L\+TE network.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK on success
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT on failure
\item sinr\+Ptr and io\+Ptr return I\+N\+T32\+\_\+\+M\+AX when the value isn\textquotesingle{}t available.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If the caller is passing a bad pointer into this function, it\textquotesingle{}s a fatal error, the function won\textquotesingle{}t return.

{\bfseries multi-\/app safe} 
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em Metrics\+Ref} & Signal metrics reference. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em ss\+Ptr} & Signal strength in d\+Bm \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em bler\+Ptr} & Block error rate \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em rsrq\+Ptr} & R\+S\+RQ value in dB as measured by L1 with 1 decimal place \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em rsrp\+Ptr} & Current R\+S\+RP in d\+Bm as measured by L1 with 1 decimal place \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em snr\+Ptr} & S\+NR level in dB with 1 decimal place (15 = 1.\+5 dB) \\
\hline

\index{le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+interface.\+h}!le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+\+Get\+Serving\+Cell\+Id@{le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+\+Get\+Serving\+Cell\+Id}}
\index{le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+\+Get\+Serving\+Cell\+Id@{le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+\+Get\+Serving\+Cell\+Id}!le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+\+Get\+Serving\+Cell\+Id(void)}{le_mrc_GetServingCellId(void)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}uint32\+\_\+t le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+\+Get\+Serving\+Cell\+Id (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{le__mrc__interface_8h_aafc9fb71c3013b7b26dc386b13ca4a85}{}\label{le__mrc__interface_8h_aafc9fb71c3013b7b26dc386b13ca4a85}
This function must be called to get the serving Cell Identifier.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The Cell Identifier. U\+I\+N\+T32\+\_\+\+M\+AX value is returned if the value is not available.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
When the module is in U\+M\+TS network, the A\+PI returns the serving U\+T\+R\+AN Cell Identity (U\+C-\/\+Id) which is used to identify the cell uniquely. It is composed of the Controlling Radio Network Controller Identifier (C\+R\+N\+C-\/\+Id, 12 bits) and the Cell Identifier (C-\/\+Id, 16 bits). (3\+G\+PP 25.\+401, section 6.\+1.\+5) The Cell Identifier is coded in the lower 2 bytes of the 4 bytes U\+C-\/\+Id and the C\+R\+N\+C-\/\+Id is coded in the upper 2 bytes. Example\+: the A\+PI returns 7807609 -\/$>$ 0x772279 (C\+R\+N\+C-\/\+Id = 0x77 , cell ID = 0x2279)

{\bfseries multi-\/app safe} 
\end{DoxyNote}

This function returns the signal metrics measured on U\+M\+TS or T\+D-\/\+S\+C\+D\+MA networks.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK on success
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT on failure
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If the caller is passing a bad pointer into this function, it\textquotesingle{}s a fatal error, the function won\textquotesingle{}t return.

{\bfseries multi-\/app safe} 
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em Metrics\+Ref} & Signal metrics reference. \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em ss\+Ptr} & Signal strength in d\+Bm \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em bler\+Ptr} & Block error rate \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em ecio\+Ptr} & Ec/\+Io value in dB with 1 decimal place (-\/15 = -\/1.\+5 dB) (Negative value) \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em rscp\+Ptr} & Measured R\+S\+CP in d\+Bm (negative value, value I\+N\+T32\+\_\+\+M\+AX means that R\+S\+CP is not available) \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt out}  & {\em sinr\+Ptr} & Measured S\+I\+NR in dB (only applicable for T\+D-\/\+S\+C\+D\+MA network, value I\+N\+T32\+\_\+\+M\+AX means that the S\+I\+NR is not available) \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Set handler called when server disconnection is detected.

When a server connection is lost, call this handler then exit with L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+T\+AL. If a program wants to continue without exiting, it should call longjmp() from inside the handler. \index{le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+interface.\+h}!le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+\+Set\+Signal\+Strength\+Ind\+Delta@{le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+\+Set\+Signal\+Strength\+Ind\+Delta}}

)}\hypertarget{le__mrc__interface_8h_a0f2b4015962c83ec9a74ee68f7b509fd}{}\label{le__mrc__interface_8h_a0f2b4015962c83ec9a74ee68f7b509fd}
This function sets a signal strength indication delta for a specific R\+AT.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK Function succeeded.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+B\+A\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER Bad parameters.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT Function failed.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The signal delta is set in units of 0.\+1 d\+Bm. For example, to set a delta of 10.\+6 d\+Bm, the delta value must be set to 106.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
The signal delta resolution is platform dependent. Please refer to platform\+Constraints\+Modem\+Radiocontrol section for full details. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em rat} & Radio Access Technology \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em delta} & Signal delta in units of 0.\+1 d\+Bm \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+interface.\+h}!le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service@{le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service}}
\index{le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service@{le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service}!le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service(void)}{le_mrc_TryConnectService(void)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf le\+\_\+result\+\_\+t} le\+\_\+mrc\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{void}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{le__mrc__interface_8h_a28d361984ad02bd619593207129c0428}{}\label{le__mrc__interface_8h_a28d361984ad02bd619593207129c0428}
Try to connect the current client thread to the service providing this A\+PI. Return with an error if the service is not available.

For each thread that wants to use this A\+PI, either Connect\+Service or Try\+Connect\+Service must be called before any other functions in this A\+PI. Normally, Connect\+Service is automatically called for the main thread, but not for any other thread. For details, see \hyperlink{apiFilesC_apiFilesC_client}{Client-\/specific Functions}.

This function is created automatically.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK if the client connected successfully to the service.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+U\+N\+A\+V\+A\+I\+L\+A\+B\+LE if the server is not currently offering the service to which the client is bound.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+M\+I\+T\+T\+ED if the client interface is not bound to any service (doesn\textquotesingle{}t have a binding).
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+M\+M\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR if the Service Directory cannot be reached. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
